Checked in online. Pretty easy. Wait time a little longer than estimate given but not too bad. Stylist was wrapping up previous client.

Steve, my stylist, was very concerned about my preferences. Asked multiple questions, cut when understood what I wanted. Pleasant conversation throughout. Did not feel rushed.

Prices are reasonable.

Shop has good COVID policy in place, in use.

Great visit.< /review>

He laughed and smirked through the entire interaction. I told him he was giving us horrible customer service and the response was "im sorry you feel that way". Never once were we offered an apology over the phone or in person. He refused to look at the pizzas stating he would do it later and acted as if we were inconveniencing them for trying to return inedible food.  He also at one point said that he was not going to put us ahead of other customer's during their rush. I'm sorry, but I have worked in food service my entire life and anytime you mess up this badly you're supposed to make it right not argue with the customer and refuse to give them a refund reciept. He also went to the back to initiate the refund and when he came out never did any transaction on the actual register.

We went to the other location in San Marcos and asked the manager there what their policy is. She stated that everything he said was absolutely untrue and that their policy is actually to give the customer the return reciept immediately because when you enter  a refund two receipts print out and one is for the customer. She was fairly confident that he didnt enter the refund.

All we wanted was a refund for delivery and tip, but he was combative from the moment we walked in. One guy in the back actually yelled "get out of here" while we were there. <Rating>5< /Rating><GmapID>0x808fcb3d87bf8903:0xc91183ebb0ccc0ba< /GmapID>< Review>
We took our baby to Dr. Ligh for a possible tongue tie and couldn't have been happier with our experience. He showed us pictures ahead of time of normal frenulums vs tied tongues, which made it clear to us that our baby was tied, then examined the baby pointing out the indicators. We opted for a release procedure after weighing pros and cons. He gave us space to ask questions and never pressured us to treat. He was supportive of us parents throughout the process--explaining things ahead of time so we felt comfortable with the treatment plan, giving thorough and easy to understand instructions for aftercare, and letting us contact him as much as needed afterwards in case we had concerns. He also allowed us to hold her during the procedure, which was comforting. We would recommend him to anyone! The only downside was that it took a couple weeks to get in for the first appointment--he is busy because he is awesome. It was worth the wait to feel the level of comfort that we had.</Review>

< text>
We came to Dr. Ligh when our baby was 9 weeks old, with a posterior tongue and lip tie.  I had been strugging with breastfeeding (mastitis, thrush, poor latch), and was very apprehensive about doing the procedure.  Dr. Ligh took the time and was very thorough in explaining the impact a tongue tie can have to breastfeeding, what the procedure entailed, and post op stretches to ensure success.  There was no pressure in the decision making, and he gave us the time we needed to consider how to move forward.  We decided to do the procedure for both the tongue and lip.  Though I'm sure he has a ton of patients, he made me feel like I was his only patient.  After the procedure he shared with me his personal number to call anytime I had concerns.  At one point he let me come to the office above a beyond what was covered by insurance to double check that the tongue had not re-attached.   He also spoke to my lactation consultant 3 times, as well as meeting with my chiropractor to ensure my daughter was making the right progress.  It really does take a team, and I'm so happy that he was part of it.  Our daughter today has good tongue elevation and movement, and we are working on improving the latch.  Slowly but surely!  I'd highly recommend Dr. Ligh--do no hesitate to at least schedule a consultation if you are struggling with breastfeeding!< /text>

< Text>
Bottom Line: Dr. Ligh is a solid guy and an expert on tongue/lip tie releases (procedure is called a frenotomy).  He is very knowledgeable when it comes to breastfeeding latch challenges caused by an infant's tongue and lip ties.  I highly recommend him to anyone needing that procedure for their infant and have already recommended him to others I've met struggling with the same issues.

Further Details:  Dr. Ligh saved my breastfeeding relationship with my son.
I went to Dr. Ligh after 9 weeks of exclusively breastfeeding my son with constant pain and trauma to me (my son was thriving the entire time, thank goodness) and on the verge of a second bout of mastitis.  Previously I had been to 2 pediatricians, 1 ENT, 5 lactation consultants and 1 dentist who each recommended holding off on releasing his lip tie (which was obvious) and misdiagnosed his tongue tie (they all said he didn't have one).  Dr. Ligh appropriately diagnosed the tongue tie (it was posterior submucosal--the hardest to diagnose) and released both tongue and lip in the office.

The frenotomy is a quick procedure (under a minute).  Dr. Ligh uses an electrocautery pen rather than a laser; it is just as effective and has the added benefit that you can hold your baby during the procedure, which was important to me.

Dr. Ligh's follow up care was also excellent.  He clearly explained the tongue and lip exercises that are necessary to prevent reattachment and then followed up to ensure the exercises were going well and the wound was healing properly.

5 stars also for Dr. Ligh's staff, especially Ernestina.  She was extremely responsive and helpful in getting us seen especially on such short notice given the worsening of my symptoms.</Text>

< review>
I had a great experience here as a first time patient! The team here is super friendly and professional (Amber, Kasey, Gayanne, and Dr. Oh) and everything is very clean. All the instruments are covered in plastic that is thrown away after use and all surfaces disinfected. They use what seems to be the latest modern equipment with high resolution digital images. It was cool getting to see my teeth from multiple angles in color. Dr. Oh felt like an old friend and was very gentle on my teeth. I didn't even need an anesthesia for the filling. I'm so glad I switched from another dentist nearby who was gruff, seemed in a rush, and told me I had over $500 in cavities whereas with Dr. Oh's team I paid only $140! Talk about being glad I switched! I don't normally write a long review or take a photo with the doctor, but I'm just that surprisingly happy with the service here!</review>

<date>1516043876614< /date>< Rating>
5< /Rating>
< Review>
This is a great little park for toddlers, preschoolers, and maybe up to about 7 for the play equipment. It only has the toddler swings though, but the rest would be fun for younger kids. It's hard to find a safe place for the little kids because most parks are designed for older kids. This is the perfect one just for those little ones! There are 2 basketball half courts for older kids and adults. Plenty of tables in the shade by the play equipment for a birthday party or lunch at the park. There is also a small parking lot to park in. The hours are 5am to 1030pm. They have park lights, but I'm not sure how well it would light up the park after dark.</Review>

<Rating>1<//Rating>< review>
This park basically sucks. Not for children for the most part. There's always cigarette butts in the play ground. The dirt that the benches are in have broken glass everywhere. The city workers come but do nothing. There's no clean up.

80% of the time I walk with my kids there, there's some teenage kids smoking weed. You can smell it. They do it with no shame and no concern for the kids in the area. I've called the cops many times and I would encourage others to do the same. This place is for the children. Not the dumbasses.

There's no bathrooms here. So if you do go, make sure your kids "go", before you leave

I will be back only because I believe the park is for children and it's up to us as parents to make a difference.<//review>
